Random XXL DAG

ID: synthetic.random_xxlarge  |  Domains: synthetic  |  Completeness: full  |  Cost Model: deterministic

Extra-extra-large random layered DAG (depth=20, width 30-70, ~1118 tasks). Largest benchmark for extreme scalability testing.
